           <h4 name="e9b3" id="e9b3" class="graf graf--h4 graf--leading">Hi, dear developers and&nbsp;readers!</h4>
           <p name="4a77" id="4a77" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">If you are interested in Open Source and are considering to join the community of Open Source developers, it is possible that in this list you will find the project that will suit you (In fact I am sure that you will find).</p>
           <p name="2be4" id="2be4" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing">Here are you can see the really big list of really interesting Open Source projects on language such as Elixir, Erlang, Haskell, Clojure, Python, Ruby, Lua, JS, Go, C++, Swift, Bash, R and etc.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

           <h3 name="7de0" id="7de0" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Emacs/Common Lisp</h3>
           <p name="6364" id="6364" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="0650" id="0650" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/magit/magit" data-href="https://github.com/magit/magit" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Magit</em></strong></a> is an interface to the version control system <a href="https://git-scm.com/" data-href="https://git-scm.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Git</a>, implemented as an <a href="https://www.gnu.org/software/emacs" data-href="https://www.gnu.org/software/emacs" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Emacs</a> package. Magit aspires to be a complete Git porcelain. While we cannot (yet) claim that Magit wraps and improves upon each and every Git command, it is complete enough to allow even experienced Git users to perform almost all of their daily version control tasks directly from within Emacs. While many fine Git clients exist, only Magit and Git itself deserve to be called porcelains. <a href="https://magit.vc/about" data-href="https://magit.vc/about" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">(more)</a></p>
           <figure name="bc4a" id="bc4a" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 168px; max-height: 200px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 119%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*kPc9uZd0tipuHwz8." data-width="168" data-height="200">

              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*kPc9uZd0tipuHwz8.">

           <p name="4a7b" id="4a7b" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/fukamachi/woo" data-href="https://github.com/fukamachi/woo" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Woo</em></strong></a> is a fast non-blocking HTTP server built on top of <a href="http://software.schmorp.de/pkg/libev.html" data-href="http://software.schmorp.de/pkg/libev.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">libev</a>. Although Woo is written in Common Lisp, it aims to be the fastest web server written in any programming language.</p>
           <p name="2785" id="2785" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">How fast?</p>
           <figure name="5999" id="5999" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="4f75" id="4f75" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/fukamachi/clack" data-href="https://github.com/fukamachi/clack" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Clack</em></strong></a> is a web application environment for Common Lisp inspired by Python’s WSGI and Ruby’s Rack.</p>
           <p name="7a10" id="7a10" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Usage:</p>
           <pre name="335d" id="335d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">(defvar *handler*<br>    (clack:clackup<br>      (lambda (env)<br>        (declare (ignore env))<br>        '(200 (:content-type "text/plain") ("Hello, Clack!")))))</pre>

           <p name="e379" id="e379" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/tonini/alchemist.el" data-href="https://github.com/tonini/alchemist.el" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Alchemist</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em></strong>an Elixir Tooling Integration Into Emacs. <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Alchemist</em> comes with a bunch of features, which are:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="4cad" id="4cad" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Mix integration</li>
            <li name="12a9" id="12a9" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Compile &amp; Execution of Elixir code</li>
            <li name="d460" id="d460" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Inline code evaluation</li>
            <li name="68db" id="68db" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Inline macro expanding</li>
            <li name="d69d" id="d69d" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Documentation lookup</li>
            <li name="1eb0" id="1eb0" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Definition lookup</li>
            <li name="70a4" id="70a4" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Powerful IEx integration</li>
            <li name="ae93" id="ae93" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Smart code completion</li>
            <li name="d095" id="d095" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Elixir project management</li>
            <li name="b690" id="b690" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Phoenix support</li>
            <li name="c685" id="c685" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Integration with <a href="http://company-mode.github.io/" data-href="http://company-mode.github.io/" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">company-mode</a></li>
           </ul>

           <h3 name="d13a" id="d13a" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Python</h3>
           <p name="e95f" id="e95f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="1d77" id="1d77" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/sobolevn/django-split-settings" data-href="https://github.com/sobolevn/django-split-settings" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">django-split-setting</strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">: </strong>Organize Django settings into multiple files and directories. Easily override and modify settings. Use wildcards and optional settings files.</p>

         <div class="section-divider">

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="c074" id="c074" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/getpelican/pelican" data-href="https://github.com/getpelican/pelican" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Pelican</em></strong></a> is a static site generator, written in <a href="http://www.python.org/" data-href="http://www.python.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Python</a>.</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="8928" id="8928" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Write content in <a href="http://docutils.sourceforge.net/rst.html" data-href="http://docutils.sourceforge.net/rst.html" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">reStructuredText</a> or <a href="http://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/" data-href="http://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown/" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Markdown</a> using your editor of choice</li>
            <li name="049a" id="049a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Includes a simple command line tool to (re)generate site files</li>
            <li name="ceb1" id="ceb1" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Easy to interface with version control systems and web hooks</li>
            <li name="7496" id="7496" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Completely static output is simple to host anywhere</li>
           </ul>
           <figure name="1862" id="1862" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--li graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 550px; max-height: 552px;">

        <section name="4bd2" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="4c90" id="4c90" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow" data-href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">tensorflow</em></strong></a>?—?an open source software library for numerical computation using data flow graphs. Nodes in the graph represent mathematical operations, while the graph edges represent the multidimensional data arrays (tensors) that flow between them. This flexible architecture lets you deploy computation to one or more CPUs or GPUs in a desktop, server, or mobile device without rewriting code. TensorFlow also includes TensorBoard, a data visualization toolkit.</p>
           <figure name="b1c0" id="b1c0" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 352px; max-height: 300px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 85.2%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*dNVUpWFLoysACE9z." data-width="352" data-height="300">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*dNVUpWFLoysACE9z.?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*dNVUpWFLoysACE9z.">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*dNVUpWFLoysACE9z.">

        <section name="edcb" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="1628" id="1628" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/magenta" data-href="https://github.com/tensorflow/magenta" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Magenta</em></strong></a> is a project from the Google Brain team that asks: Can we use machine learning to create compelling art and music? If so, how? If not, why not? We’ll use TensorFlow, and we’ll release our models and tools in open source on this GitHub. We’ll also post demos, tutorial blog postings, and technical papers. If you’d like to keep up on Magenta as it grows, you can read our blog and or join our discussion group.</p>
           <figure name="98fb" id="98fb" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 525px;">

             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*t_d8YHfohBitJc-T.png" data-width="867" data-height="650" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*t_d8YHfohBitJc-T.png">

        <section name="52d3" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="c553" id="c553" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/numenta/nupic" data-href="https://github.com/numenta/nupic" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">The Numenta Platform for Intelligent Computing (NUPIC)</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em"> </em></strong>is a machine intelligence platform that implements the <a href="http://numenta.com/learn/hierarchical-temporal-memory-white-paper.html" data-href="http://numenta.com/learn/hierarchical-temporal-memory-white-paper.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">HTM learning algorithms</a>. HTM is a detailed computational theory of the neocortex. At the core of HTM are time-based continuous learning algorithms that store and recall spatial and temporal patterns. NuPIC is suited to a variety of problems, particularly anomaly detection and prediction of streaming data sources.</p>
           <figure name="ca30" id="ca30" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 128px; max-height: 128px;">

           <p name="828c" id="828c" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/eliangcs/http-prompt" data-href="https://github.com/eliangcs/http-prompt" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">http-prompt</em></strong></a>?—?an interactive command-line HTTP client featuring autocomplete and syntax highlighting.</p>

        <section name="f5fb" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="4369" id="4369" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/gabrielfalcao/HTTPretty" data-href="https://github.com/gabrielfalcao/HTTPretty" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">HTTPretty</em></strong></a>?—?HTTP client mocking tool for Python, it’s like ruby’s FakeWeb for python.</p>
           <p name="b619" id="b619" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Usage:</p>
           <pre name="37c1" id="37c1" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import requests<br>import httpretty</pre>
           <pre name="f421" id="f421" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">def test_one():<br>    httpretty.enable()  # enable HTTPretty so that it will monkey patch the socket module<br>    httpretty.register_uri(httpretty.GET, "http://yipit.com/",<br>                           body="Find the best daily deals")</pre>
           <pre name="fe0b" id="fe0b" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    response = requests.get('http://yipit.com')</pre>
           <pre name="771a" id="771a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    assert response.text == "Find the best daily deals"</pre>
           <pre name="8d58" id="8d58" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">    httpretty.disable()  # disable afterwards, so that you will have no problems in code that uses that socket module<br>    httpretty.reset()    # reset HTTPretty state (clean up registered urls and request history)</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="f860" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="91a4" id="91a4" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/falconry/falcon" data-href="https://github.com/falconry/falcon" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">falcon</em></strong></a>?—?is a <a href="http://falconframework.org/index.html" data-href="http://falconframework.org/index.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">high-performance Python framework</a> for building cloud APIs. It encourages the REST architectural style, and tries to do as little as possible while remaining <a href="http://falconframework.org/index.html#Benefits" data-href="http://falconframework.org/index.html#Benefits" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">highly effective</a>.</p>
           <figure name="19b8" id="19b8" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 253px; max-height: 380px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 150.2%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*q9KGh0C5nrVelow1.png" data-width="253" data-height="380">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*q9KGh0C5nrVelow1.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*q9KGh0C5nrVelow1.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*q9KGh0C5nrVelow1.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="640a" id="640a" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Example:</p>
           <pre name="cdbb" id="cdbb" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">import</strong> <strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">falcon</strong><br><br></pre>
           <pre name="b58e" id="b58e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"><em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># Falcon follows the REST architectural style, meaning (among</em><br><em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># other things) that you think in terms of resources and state</em><br><em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># transitions, which map to HTTP verbs.</em><br><strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">class</strong> <strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">ThingsResource</strong>(object):<br>    <strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">def</strong> on_get(self, req, resp):<br>        <em class="markup--em markup--pre-em">"""Handles GET requests"""</em><br>        resp.status = falcon.HTTP_200  <em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># This is the default status</em><br>        resp.body = ('<strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">\n</strong>Two things awe me most, the starry sky '<br>                     'above me and the moral law within me.<strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">\n</strong>'<br>                     '<strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">\n</strong>'<br>                     '    ~ Immanuel Kant<strong class="markup--strong markup--pre-strong">\n\n</strong>')</pre>
           <pre name="fbb7" id="fbb7" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"><em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># falcon.API instances are callable WSGI apps</em><br>app = falcon.API()</pre>
           <pre name="bc1a" id="bc1a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"><em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># Resources are represented by long-lived class instances</em><br>things = ThingsResource()</pre>
           <pre name="88bb" id="88bb" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing"><em class="markup--em markup--pre-em"># things will handle all requests to the '/things' URL path</em><br>app.add_route('/things', things)</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="7734" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="b679" id="b679" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/nicolaiarocci/eve" data-href="https://github.com/nicolaiarocci/eve" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">eve</a>?—?an open source Python REST API framework designed for human beings. It allows to effortlessly build and deploy highly customizable, fully featured RESTful Web Services.</p>
           <p name="1ccb" id="1ccb" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Eve is powered by Flask, Redis, Cerberus, Events and offers support for both MongoDB and SQL backends.</p>
           <pre name="c2c1" id="c2c1" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">from eve import Eve</pre>
           <pre name="1b0b" id="1b0b" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">app = Eve()<br>app.run()</pre>
           <p name="9009" id="9009" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">The API is now live, ready to be consumed:</p>
           <pre name="203c" id="203c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">$ curl -i <a href="http://example.com/people" data-href="http://example.com/people" class="markup--anchor markup--pre-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">http://example.com/people</a><br>HTTP/1.1 200 OK</pre>
          </div>
         </div>

        <section name="fec6" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="88a5" id="88a5" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/lk-geimfari/mimesis" data-href="https://github.com/lk-geimfari/mimesis" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Mimesis</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em"> </em></strong>is a fast and easier to use Python library for generate dummy data. These data are very useful when you need to bootstrap the database in the testing phase of your software. A great example of how you can use the library is a web applications on Flask or Django which need a data, such as users (email, username, name, surname etc.), posts (tags, text, title, publishing date and etc.) asf. The library use the JSON files as a datastore and doesn’t have any dependencies. The library offers more than 18 different data providers (from the personal to transport and not only).</p>
           <figure name="7ac2" id="7ac2" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 500px; max-height: 253px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 50.6%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*bZtdscI2dXuTz5s-.png" data-width="500" data-height="253">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*bZtdscI2dXuTz5s-.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*bZtdscI2dXuTz5s-.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*bZtdscI2dXuTz5s-.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="3d87" id="3d87" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Below you can see, how to generate fake paths using <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Mimesis</code>:</p>
           <pre name="a787" id="a787" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&gt;&gt;&gt; from m<code class="markup--code markup--pre-code">imesis</code> import Path<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; path = Path()</pre>
           <pre name="4d78" id="4d78" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; path.root<br>'/'</pre>
           <pre name="ec86" id="ec86" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; path.home<br>'/home/'</pre>
           <pre name="2ce0" id="2ce0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; path.user(gender='female')<br>'/home/chieko'</pre>
           <pre name="ea08" id="ea08" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; path.users_folder(user_gender='male')<br>'/home/lyndon/Documents'</pre>
           <pre name="5ca4" id="5ca4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; path.dev_dir(user_gender='female')<br>'/home/edra/Development/Ruby'</pre>
           <pre name="9254" id="9254" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; path.project_dir(user_gender='female')<br>'/home/katharina/Development/C Shell/litany'</pre>
           <p name="f175" id="f175" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">or how to generate dummy model of transport:</p>
           <pre name="46a1" id="46a1" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&gt;&gt;&gt; from m<code class="markup--code markup--pre-code">imesis</code> import Transport<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; transport = Transport()</pre>
           <pre name="5faa" id="5faa" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; transport.truck()<br>'Union-0632 FX'</pre>
           <pre name="7f19" id="7f19" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; transport.truck(model_mask="##/@")<br>'Jiaotong-78/P'</pre>
           <pre name="4c61" id="4c61" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; transport.car()<br>'Pontiac Grand Am'</pre>
           <pre name="8c1d" id="8c1d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; transport.airplane()<br>'Boeing 575'</pre>
           <pre name="30c4" id="30c4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">&gt;&gt;&gt; transport.airplane(model_mask="7##")<br>'Airbus 778'</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="0ea4" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="db63" id="db63" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/lk-geimfari/expynent" data-href="https://github.com/lk-geimfari/expynent" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">expynent</em></strong></a>?—?a library that provides regex patterns for Python. If you hate to write regular expressions, then expynent can help you. Examples are below.</p>
           <p name="87a1" id="87a1" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Just import the pattern that you wanna use:</p>
           <pre name="08f2" id="08f2" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import re<br>import expynent.patterns as expas</pre>
           <pre name="f190" id="f190" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">if re.match(expas.ZIP_CODE['RU'], '43134'):<br>    print('match')<br>else:<br>    print('not match')</pre>
           <pre name="402b" id="402b" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># Output: 'not match'</pre>
           <p name="2f41" id="2f41" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">also you can use compiled patterns:</p>
           <pre name="d5c0" id="d5c0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">from expynent.compiled import username</pre>
           <pre name="cbd0" id="cbd0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">u = input('Enter username: ')</pre>
           <pre name="5c66" id="5c66" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">if username.match(u):<br>    print('valid')<br>else:<br>    print('invalid')</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

        <section name="a545" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="a7ca" id="a7ca" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/sdispater/pendulum" data-href="https://github.com/sdispater/pendulum" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">pendulum</em></strong></a><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em>Python datetimes made easy.</p>
           <p name="b7ac" id="b7ac" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Usage:</p>
           <pre name="2bd7" id="2bd7" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&gt;&gt;&gt; import pendulum</pre>
           <pre name="d590" id="d590" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; now_in_paris = pendulum.now('Europe/Paris')<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; now_in_paris<br>'2016-07-04T00:49:58.502116+02:00'</pre>
           <pre name="2f13" id="2f13" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># Seamless timezone switching<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; now_in_paris.in_timezone('UTC')<br>'2016-07-03T22:49:58.502116+00:00'</pre>
           <pre name="516d" id="516d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; tomorrow = pendulum.now().add(days=1)<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; last_week = pendulum.now().subtract(weeks=1)</pre>
           <pre name="2ffa" id="2ffa" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; if pendulum.now().is_weekend():<br>...     print('Party!')<br>'Party!'</pre>
           <pre name="78fe" id="78fe" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; past = pendulum.now().subtract(minutes=2)<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; past.diff_for_humans()<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; '2 minutes ago'</pre>
           <pre name="1dc2" id="1dc2" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt;&gt;&gt; delta = past - last_week<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; delta.hours<br>23<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; delta.in_words(locale='en')<br>'6 days 23 hours 58 minutes'</pre>
           <pre name="6bff" id="6bff" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># Proper handling of datetime normalization<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; pendulum.create(2013, 3, 31, 2, 30, 0, 0, 'Europe/Paris')<br>'2013-03-31T03:30:00+02:00' # 2:30 does not exist (Skipped time)</pre>
           <pre name="fe67" id="fe67" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing"># Proper handling of dst transitions<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; just_before = pendulum.create(2013, 3, 31, 1, 59, 59, 999999, 'Europe/Paris')<br>'2013-03-31T01:59:59.999999+01:00'<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; just_before.add(microseconds=1)<br>'2013-03-31T03:00:00+02:00'</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="5f8e" id="5f8e" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/airbnb/superset" data-href="https://github.com/airbnb/superset" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">superset</em></strong></a>?—?a data exploration platform designed to be visual, intuitive and interactive.</p>

          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="e24b" id="e24b" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/gruns/furl" data-href="https://github.com/gruns/furl" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">furl</em></strong></a><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em>a small Python library that makes manipulating URLs simple.</p>
           <p name="17bb" id="17bb" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Example:</p>
           <pre name="8970" id="8970" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">&gt;&gt;&gt; from furl import furl<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; f = furl('http://www.google.com/?one=1&amp;two=2')<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; f.args['three'] = '3'<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; del f.args['one']<br>&gt;&gt;&gt; f.url<br>'http://www.google.com/?two=2&amp;three=3'</pre>

           <p name="5a5c" id="5a5c" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/jkbrzt/httpie" data-href="https://github.com/jkbrzt/httpie" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">httpie</em></strong></a><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em>a command line HTTP client. Its goal is to make CLI interaction with web services as human-friendly as possible. It provides a simple <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">http</code> command that allows for sending arbitrary HTTP requests using a simple and natural syntax, and displays colorized output. HTTPie can be used for testing, debugging, and generally interacting with HTTP servers.</p>

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="8e7a" id="8e7a" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Lua</h3>
           <p name="8dd4" id="8dd4" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="968e" id="968e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing"><a href="https://github.com/leafo/moonscript" data-href="https://github.com/leafo/moonscript" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">moonscript</em></strong></a>?—?a programmer friendly language that compiles into <a href="http://www.lua.org/" data-href="http://www.lua.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Lua</a>. It gives you the power of the fastest scripting language combined with a rich set of features. It runs on Lua 5.1 and above, including alternative runtimes like LuaJIT.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="c2ff" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <figure name="0979" id="0979" class="graf graf--figure graf--leading graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 637px; max-height: 346px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 54.300000000000004%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*-ytpHKPWbcBnOpVd." data-width="637" data-height="346">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*-ytpHKPWbcBnOpVd.?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*-ytpHKPWbcBnOpVd.">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*-ytpHKPWbcBnOpVd.">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="fd79" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="c7da" id="c7da" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/kikito/middleclass" data-href="https://github.com/kikito/middleclass" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">middleclass</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em></strong>a simple OOP library for Lua. It has inheritance, metamethods (operators), class variables and weak mixin support.</p>
           <p name="e410" id="e410" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Quick look:</p>
           <pre name="9564" id="9564" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">local class = require 'middleclass'</pre>
           <pre name="d59f" id="d59f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">local Fruit = class('Fruit') -- 'Fruit' is the class' name</pre>
           <pre name="8160" id="8160" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">function Fruit:initialize(sweetness)<br>  self.sweetness = sweetness<br>end</pre>
           <pre name="5383" id="5383" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">Fruit.static.sweetness_threshold = 5 -- class variable (also admits methods)</pre>
           <pre name="edb6" id="edb6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">function Fruit:isSweet()<br>  return self.sweetness &gt; Fruit.sweetness_threshold<br>end</pre>
           <pre name="777f" id="777f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">local Lemon = class('Lemon', Fruit) -- subclassing</pre>
           <pre name="4b11" id="4b11" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">function Lemon:initialize()<br>  Fruit.initialize(self, 1) -- invoking the superclass' initializer<br>end</pre>
           <pre name="9af8" id="9af8" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">local lemon = Lemon:new()</pre>
           <pre name="8e3a" id="8e3a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">print(lemon:isSweet()) -- false</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="028d" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="ee68" id="ee68" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/luarocks/luarocks" data-href="https://github.com/luarocks/luarocks" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">luarocks</em></strong></a>?—?a package manager for Lua modules.</p>
           <figure name="1f96" id="1f96" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 171px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 24.4%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*sawSUbg8SqRSpEha." data-width="739" data-height="180" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*sawSUbg8SqRSpEha.">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*sawSUbg8SqRSpEha.?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>

               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*sawSUbg8SqRSpEha.">
              </noscript>
             </div>

           </figure>

        <section name="7f2d" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="ecb3" id="ecb3" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/fcambus/telize" data-href="https://github.com/fcambus/telize" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">telize</em></strong></a>?—?a REST API built on Nginx and Lua allowing to get a visitor IP address and to query location information from any IP address. It outputs JSON-encoded IP geolocation data, and supports both JSON and JSONP.</p>
           <pre name="4860" id="4860" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing"><code class="markup--code markup--pre-code">t  e  l  i  z  e<br>                       _______________________<br>                 ______\                     /_______<br>                \\     \\           ___     //      /<br>           __    \ ____  \   __    /   \   _____/\ / ____<br>       ___/  \____/  _//____/  \___\___/___\__   /__/  _//____<br>      \\__    ____  __/  __     __      ____    ____  __/  __///<br>        /      \_   |/    \_     /       \/     /_/   |/    \_<br>      \\\   ___/\___       /____/\_______/\   ___/\___       /<br>  &lt;0(--- \__/ -h7- \______/   \       .    \__/ ---- \______/ --(0&gt;<br>                       \      .\     /.      .<br>                        \      .\   //      /<br>                         \______\\ //______/<br>                                  Y</code></pre>

           <h3 name="22bb" id="22bb" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Golang</h3>
           <p name="1907" id="1907" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="0fee" id="0fee" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/cayleygraph/cayley" data-href="https://github.com/cayleygraph/cayley" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Cayley</em></strong></a> is an open-source graph inspired by the graph database behind <a href="http://freebase.com/" data-href="http://freebase.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Freebase</a> and Google’s <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knowledge_Graph" data-href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knowledge_Graph" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Knowledge Graph</a>.</p>
           <p name="ffc9" id="ffc9" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Its goal is to be a part of the developer’s toolbox where <a href="http://linkeddata.org/" data-href="http://linkeddata.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Linked Data</a> and graph-shaped data (semantic webs, social networks, etc) in general are concerned.</p>
           <figure name="55d1" id="55d1" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 190px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 27.1%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*LT_0dZDhKD2Mve9r." data-width="1195" data-height="324" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*LT_0dZDhKD2Mve9r.">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*LT_0dZDhKD2Mve9r.?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>

        <section name="2371" class="section section--body">

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="33dc" id="33dc" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes" data-href="https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Kubernetes</em></strong></a> is an open source system for managing <a href="http://kubernetes.io/docs/whatisk8s/" data-href="http://kubernetes.io/docs/whatisk8s/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">containerized applications</a> across multiple hosts, providing basic mechanisms for deployment, maintenance, and scaling of applications. Kubernetes is hosted by the Cloud Native Computing Foundation.</p>
           <p name="b032" id="b032" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Kubernetes builds upon a decade and a half of experience at Google running production workloads at scale using a system called <a href="https://research.google.com/pubs/pub43438.html" data-href="https://research.google.com/pubs/pub43438.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Borg</a>, combined with best-of-breed ideas and practices from the community.</p>
           <figure name="e79e" id="e79e" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 679px;">

           <pre name="a465" id="a465" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">func main() {<br>    img, err := imgio.Open("filename.jpg")<br>    if err != nil {<br>        panic(err)<br>    }</pre>
           <pre name="97bc" id="97bc" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    inverted := effect.Invert(img)<br>    resized := transform.Resize(inverted, 800, 800, transform.Linear)<br>    rotated := transform.Rotate(resized, 45, nil)</pre>
           <pre name="c4ca" id="c4ca" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">    if err := imgio.Save("filename", rotated, imgio.PNG); err != nil {<br>        panic(err)<br>    }<br>}</pre>

           <p name="74e3" id="74e3" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/derekparker/delve" data-href="https://github.com/derekparker/delve" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">delve</em></strong></a>?—?a debugger for the Go programming language. The goal of the project is to provide a simple, full featured debugging tool for Go. Delve should be easy to invoke and easy to use. Chances are if you’re using a debugger, most likely things aren’t going your way. With that in mind, Delve should stay out of your way as much as possible.</p>

           <p name="c24e" id="c24e" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/tidwall/tile38" data-href="https://github.com/tidwall/tile38" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">tile38</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?</em></strong><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">—?</em>an open source, in-memory geolocation data store, spatial index, and realtime geofence. It supports a variety of object types including lat/lon points, bounding boxes, XYZ tiles, Geohashes, and GeoJSON.</p>
           <figure name="11d2" id="11d2" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 700px;">

           <h3 name="04ec" id="04ec" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Erlang/Elixir</h3>
           <p name="10ed" id="10ed" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="35bc" id="35bc" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/ninenines/cowboy" data-href="https://github.com/ninenines/cowboy" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">cowboy</em></strong></a>?—?a small, fast and modern HTTP server for Erlang/OTP. I think that everyone who interested in Erlang heard about a cowboy.</p>
           <figure name="9cfc" id="9cfc" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 938px;">

             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*8JmIjyHiSdA54gsv." data-width="844" data-height="1131" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*8JmIjyHiSdA54gsv.">

        <section name="9000" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="2350" id="2350" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/ChicagoBoss/ChicagoBoss" data-href="https://github.com/ChicagoBoss/ChicagoBoss" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">ChicagoBoss</em></strong></a>?—?a server framework inspired by Rails and written in Erlang. It offers all the conveniences of modern web development, including Comet. What sets Chicago Boss apart from other non-Erlang frameworks is that it can handle large amounts of traffic without any drop in performance. What sets Chicago Boss apart from other Erlang frameworks is that it is easy to set up and use.</p>

        <section name="3067" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="3bc7" id="3bc7" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/ueberauth/guardian" data-href="https://github.com/ueberauth/guardian" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">guardian</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em></strong>an authentication framework for use with Elixir applications.</p>
           <p name="5e04" id="5e04" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Guardian is based on similar ideas to Warden but is re-imagined for modern systems where Elixir manages the authentication requirements.</p>
           <p name="33ad" id="33ad" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Guardian remains a functional system. It integrates with Plug, but can be used outside of it. If you’re implementing a TCP/UDP protocol directly, or want to utilize your authentication via channels, Guardian is your friend.</p>
           <p name="f998" id="f998" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing">The core currency of authentication in Guardian is <a href="https://jwt.io/" data-href="https://jwt.io/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">JSON Web Tokens</a> (JWT). You can use the JWT to authenticate web endpoints, channels, and TCP sockets and it can contain any authenticated assertions that the issuer wants to include.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

        <section name="9475" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="7140" id="7140" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/elixir-maru/maru" data-href="https://github.com/elixir-maru/maru" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">maru</em></strong></a>?—?Elixir RESTful Framework</p>
           <p name="7203" id="7203" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Usage:</p>
           <pre name="4999" id="4999" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">defmodule Router.User do<br>  use Maru.Router</pre>
           <pre name="5483" id="5483" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  namespace :user do<br>    route_param :id do<br>      get do<br>        json(conn, %{ user: params[:id] })<br>      end</pre>
           <pre name="5bd4" id="5bd4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">      desc "description"<br>      params do<br>        requires :age,    type: Integer, values: 18..65<br>        requires :gender, type: Atom, values: [:male, :female], default: :female<br>        group    :name,   type: Map do<br>          requires :first_name<br>          requires :last_name<br>        end<br>        optional :intro,  type: String, regexp: ~r/^[a-z]+$/<br>        optional :avatar, type: File<br>        optional :avatar_url, type: String<br>        exactly_one_of [:avatar, :avatar_url]<br>      end<br>      post do<br>        ...<br>      end<br>    end<br>  end<br>end</pre>
           <pre name="b3ea" id="b3ea" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">defmodule Router.Homepage do<br>  use Maru.Router</pre>
           <pre name="6036" id="6036" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  resources do<br>    get do<br>      json(conn, %{ hello: :world })<br>    end</pre>
           <pre name="dd46" id="dd46" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    mount Router.User<br>  end<br>end<br><br></pre>
           <pre name="a6e7" id="a6e7" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">defmodule MyAPP.API do<br>  use Maru.Router</pre>
           <pre name="c6ba" id="c6ba" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  before do<br>    plug Plug.Logger<br>    plug Plug.Static, at: "/static", from: "/my/static/path/"<br>  end</pre>
           <pre name="0c48" id="0c48" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  plug Plug.Parsers,<br>    pass: ["*/*"],<br>    json_decoder: Poison,<br>    parsers: [:urlencoded, :json, :multipart]</pre>
           <pre name="06df" id="06df" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  mount Router.Homepage</pre>
           <pre name="bc37" id="bc37" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  rescue_from Unauthorized, as: e do<br>    IO.inspect e</pre>
           <pre name="7a5c" id="7a5c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    conn<br>    |&gt; put_status(401)<br>    |&gt; text("Unauthorized")<br>  end</pre>
           <pre name="9917" id="9917" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  rescue_from [MatchError, RuntimeError], with: :custom_error</pre>
           <pre name="474e" id="474e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  rescue_from :all do<br>    conn<br>    |&gt; put_status(500)<br>    |&gt; text("Server Error")<br>  end</pre>
           <pre name="05d5" id="05d5" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  defp custom_error(conn, exception) do<br>    conn<br>    |&gt; put_status(500)<br>    |&gt; text(exception.message)<br>  end<br>end</pre>
           <p name="30f5" id="30f5" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">then add the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">maru</code> to your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">config/config.exs</code></p>
           <pre name="7c25" id="7c25" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">config :maru, MyAPP.API,<br>  http: [port: 8880]</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="051b" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="56df" id="56df" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/HashNuke/hound" data-href="https://github.com/HashNuke/hound" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">hound</em></strong></a>?—?Elixir library for writing integration tests and browser automation.</p>
           <p name="32ca" id="32ca" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">ExUnit example:</p>
           <pre name="007d" id="007d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">defmodule HoundTest do<br>  use ExUnit.Case<br>  use Hound.Helpers</pre>
           <pre name="a2d5" id="a2d5" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">hound_session</pre>
           <pre name="f8f8" id="f8f8" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">test "the truth", meta do<br>    navigate_to("http://example.com/guestbook.html")</pre>
           <pre name="5ae1" id="5ae1" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">element = find_element(:name, "message")<br>    fill_field(element, "Happy Birthday ~!")<br>    submit_element(element)</pre>
           <pre name="d0ad" id="d0ad" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">assert page_title() == "Thank you"<br>  end</pre>
           <pre name="ebfe" id="ebfe" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">end</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="f3cd" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="b7d8" id="b7d8" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/bitwalker/distillery" data-href="https://github.com/bitwalker/distillery" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">distillery</em></strong></a>?—?a pure Elixir implementation of release packaging functionality for the Erlang VM (BEAM).</p>
           <p name="d03a" id="d03a" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Every alchemist requires good tools, and one of the greatest tools in the alchemist’s disposal is the distillery. The purpose of the distillery is to take something and break it down to it’s component parts, reassembling it into something better, more powerful. That is exactly what this project does?—?it takes your Mix project and produces an Erlang/OTP release, a distilled form of your raw application’s components; a single package which can be deployed anywhere, independently of an Erlang/Elixir installation. No dependencies, no hassle.</p>
           <p name="4710" id="4710" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing">This is a pure-Elixir, dependency-free implementation of release generation for Elixir projects. It is currently a standalone package, but may be integrated into Mix at some point in the future.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="92ed" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="b3de" id="b3de" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/bitwalker/timex" data-href="https://github.com/bitwalker/timex" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">timex</em></strong></a>?—?a rich, comprehensive Date/Time library for Elixir projects, with full timezone support via the&nbsp;<code class="markup--code markup--p-code">:tzdata</code> package. If you need to manipulate dates, times, datetimes, timestamps, etc., then Timex is for you! It is very easy to use Timex types in place of default Erlang types, as well as Ecto types via the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">timex_ecto</code> package.</p>
           <p name="9938" id="9938" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Here’s a few simple examples:</p>
           <pre name="cf6e" id="cf6e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&gt; use Timex<br>&gt; Timex.today<br>~D[2016-02-29]</pre>
           <pre name="42ce" id="42ce" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; datetime = Timex.now<br>#&lt;DateTime(2016-02-29T12:30:30.120+00:00Z Etc/UTC)</pre>
           <pre name="a078" id="a078" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timex.now("America/Chicago")<br>#&lt;DateTime(2016-02-29T06:30:30.120-06:00 America/Chicago)</pre>
           <pre name="2edd" id="2edd" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Duration.now<br>#&lt;Duration(P46Y6M24DT21H57M33.977711S)&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="9f53" id="9f53" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; {:ok, default_str} = Timex.format(datetime, "{ISO:Extended}")<br>{:ok, "2016-02-29T12:30:30.120+00:00"}</pre>
           <pre name="7e33" id="7e33" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; {:ok, relative_str} = Timex.shift(datetime, minutes: -3) |&gt; Timex.format("{relative}", :relative)<br>{:ok, "3 minutes ago"}</pre>
           <pre name="1189" id="1189" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; strftime_str = Timex.format!(datetime, "%FT%T%:z", :strftime)<br>"2016-02-29T12:30:30+00:00"</pre>
           <pre name="5458" id="5458" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timex.parse(default_str, "{ISO:Extended}")<br>{:ok, #&lt;DateTime(2016-02-29T12:30:30.120+00:00 Etc/Utc)}</pre>
           <pre name="213e" id="213e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timex.parse!(strftime_str, "%FT%T%:z", :strftime)<br>#&lt;DateTime(2016-02-29T12:30:30.120+00:00 Etc/Utc)</pre>
           <pre name="41c6" id="41c6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Duration.diff(Duration.now, Duration.zero, :days)<br>16850</pre>
           <pre name="c5df" id="c5df" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timex.shift(date, days: 3)<br>~D[2016-03-03]</pre>
           <pre name="7402" id="7402" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timex.shift(datetime, hours: 2, minutes: 13)<br>#&lt;DateTime(2016-02-29T14:43:30.120Z Etc/UTC)&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="1007" id="1007" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; timezone = Timezone.get("America/Chicago", Timex.now)<br>#&lt;TimezoneInfo(America/Chicago - CDT (-06:00:00))&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="58bf" id="58bf" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timezone.convert(datetime, timezone)<br>#&lt;DateTime(2016-02-29T06:30:30.120-06:00 America/Chicago)&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="e872" id="e872" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&gt; Timex.before?(Timex.today, Timex.shift(Timex.today, days: 1))<br>true</pre>
           <pre name="832f" id="832f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">&gt; Timex.before?(Timex.shift(Timex.today, days: 1), Timex.today)<br>false</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="2b8f" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="8577" id="8577" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/myfreeweb/httpotion" data-href="https://github.com/myfreeweb/httpotion" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">httpotion</em></strong></a>?—?an HTTP client for <a href="http://elixir-lang.org/" data-href="http://elixir-lang.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Elixir</a>, based on <a href="https://github.com/cmullaparthi/ibrowse" data-href="https://github.com/cmullaparthi/ibrowse" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">ibrowse</a>. Continues the HTTPun tradition of <a href="https://github.com/jnunemaker/httparty" data-href="https://github.com/jnunemaker/httparty" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">HTTParty</a>, <a href="https://github.com/gabrielfalcao/HTTPretty" data-href="https://github.com/gabrielfalcao/HTTPretty" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">HTTPretty</a>, <a href="https://github.com/edgurgel/httparrot" data-href="https://github.com/edgurgel/httparrot" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">HTTParrot</a> and <a href="https://github.com/jkbr/httpie" data-href="https://github.com/jkbr/httpie" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">HTTPie</a>.</p>
           <p name="941e" id="941e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Some basic examples:</p>
           <pre name="0527" id="0527" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">iex&gt; response = HTTPotion.get "httpbin.org/get"<br>%HTTPotion.Response{body: "...", headers: [Connection: "keep-alive", ...], status_code: 200}</pre>
           <pre name="4eaf" id="4eaf" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">iex&gt; HTTPotion.Response.success?(response)<br>true</pre>
           <pre name="93f6" id="93f6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># HTTPotion also supports querystrings like<br>iex&gt; HTTPotion.get("httpbin.org/get", query: %{page: 2})<br>%HTTPotion.Response{body: "...", headers: [Connection: "keep-alive", ...], status_code: 200}</pre>
           <pre name="fead" id="fead" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># Form data<br>iex&gt; HTTPotion.post "https://httpbin.org/post", [body: "hello=" &lt;&gt; URI.encode_www_form("w o r l d !!"),<br>  headers: ["User-Agent": "My App", "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"]]<br>%HTTPotion.Response{body: "...", headers: [Connection: "keep-alive", ...], status_code: 200}</pre>
           <pre name="1381" id="1381" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">iex&gt; HTTPotion.request :propfind, "http://httpbin.org/post", [body: "I have no idea what I'm doing"]<br>%HTTPotion.Response{body: "...", headers: [Connection: "keep-alive", ...], status_code: 405}</pre>
           <pre name="872f" id="872f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">iex&gt; HTTPotion.get "httpbin.org/basic-auth/foo/bar", [basic_auth: {"foo", "bar"}]<br>%HTTPotion.Response{body: "...", headers: ["Access-Control-Allow-Credentials": "true", ...], status_code: 200}</pre>
           <pre name="f74f" id="f74f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># Passing options to ibrowse (note that it usually takes char_lists, not elixir strings)<br>iex&gt; HTTPotion.get "http://ip6.me", [ ibrowse: [ proxy_host: 'fc81:6134:ba6c:8458:c99f:6c01:6472:8f1e', proxy_port: 8118 ] ]<br>%HTTPotion.Response{body: "...", headers: [Connection: "keep-alive", ...], status_code: 200}</pre>
           <pre name="c662" id="c662" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># The default timeout is 5000 ms, but can be changed<br>iex&gt; HTTPotion.get "http://example.com", [timeout: 10_000]</pre>
           <pre name="7251" id="7251" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># If there is an error a `HTTPotion.ErrorResponse` is returned<br>iex&gt; HTTPotion.get "http://localhost:1"<br>%HTTPotion.ErrorResponse{message: "econnrefused"}</pre>
           <pre name="bab8" id="bab8" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing"># You can also raise `HTTPError` with the `bang` version of request<br>iex&gt; HTTPotion.get! "http://localhost:1"<br>** (HTTPotion.HTTPError) econnrefused</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

           <p name="e502" id="e502" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/smpallen99/ex_admin" data-href="https://github.com/smpallen99/ex_admin" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">ex_admin</em></strong></a>?—?an add on for an application using the <a href="http://www.phoenixframework.org/" data-href="http://www.phoenixframework.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Phoenix Framework</a> to create an CRUD administration tool with little or no code.         <section name="025c" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="8a42" id="8a42" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/devinus/poison" data-href="https://github.com/devinus/poison" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">poison</em></strong></a>?—?a new JSON library for Elixir focusing on wicked-fast speed without sacrificing simplicity, completeness, or correctness.</p>
           <p name="a9e6" id="a9e6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Usage:</p>
           <pre name="3368" id="3368" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">defmodule Person do<br>  @derive [Poison.Encoder]<br>  defstruct [:name, :age]<br>end<br><br>Poison.encode!(%Person{name: "Devin Torres", age: 27})<br>#=&gt; "{\"name\":\"Devin Torres\",\"age\":27}"<br><br>Poison.decode!(~s({"name": "Devin Torres", "age": 27}), as: %Person{})<br>#=&gt; %Person{name: "Devin Torres", age: 27}<br><br>Poison.decode!(~s({"people": [{"name": "Devin Torres", "age": 27}]}),<br>  as: %{"people" =&gt; [%Person{}]})<br>#=&gt; %{"people" =&gt; [%Person{age: 27, name: "Devin Torres"}]}</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="c3d4" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="a777" id="a777" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix" data-href="https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">phoenix</em></strong></a>?—?Productive. Reliable. Fast. A productive web framework that<br>does not compromise speed and maintainability (seems that’s true).</p>
           <figure name="e57b" id="e57b" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 95px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 13.600000000000001%;"></div>
             <img class="graf-image" data-image-id="0*p8tLGfZhbLweYs4C.png" data-width="728" data-height="99" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*p8tLGfZhbLweYs4C.png" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*p8tLGfZhbLweYs4C.png">
            </div>

        <section name="8f7f" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="1f98" id="1f98" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/sugar-framework/sugar" data-href="https://github.com/sugar-framework/sugar" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Sugar</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em"> </em></strong>is a modular web framework for Elixir.</p>
           <p name="b2c3" id="b2c3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Goals:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="9caa" id="9caa" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Speed. Sugar shouldn’t be slow and neither should your project.</li>
            <li name="2ff8" id="2ff8" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Ease. Sugar should be simple because simple is easy to learn, use and maintain.</li>
            <li name="5b6b" id="5b6b" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Effective. Sugar should aid development. You have better things to which to devote your time.</li>
           </ul>
           <p name="cb3b" id="cb3b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">Example:</p>
           <pre name="b7e7" id="b7e7" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">defmodule Router do<br>  use Sugar.Router<br><br>  get "/", Hello, :index<br>  get "/pages/:id", Hello, :show<br>  post "/pages", Hello, :create<br>  put "/pages/:id" when id == 1, Hello, :show<br>end</pre>
           <figure name="5779" id="5779" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--pre graf--trailing">

           <h3 name="45bf" id="45bf" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Ruby</h3>
           <p name="b039" id="b039" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="a9af" id="a9af" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/jnunemaker/httparty" data-href="https://github.com/jnunemaker/httparty" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">httparty</em></strong></a>?—?Makes http fun again!</p>
           <p name="d3ef" id="d3ef" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Example:</p>
           <pre name="be71" id="be71" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p"># Use the class methods to get down to business quickly<br>response = HTTParty.get('http://api.stackexchange.com/2.2/questions?site=stackoverflow')</pre>
           <pre name="3470" id="3470" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">puts response.body, response.code, response.message, response.headers.inspect</pre>
           <pre name="be11" id="be11" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre"># Or wrap things up in your own class<br>class StackExchange<br>  include HTTParty<br>  base_uri 'api.stackexchange.com'</pre>
           <pre name="88a9" id="88a9" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">def initialize(service, page)<br>    @options = { query: { site: service, page: page } }<br>  end</pre>
           <pre name="fdc6" id="fdc6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">def questions<br>    self.class.get("/2.2/questions", @options)<br>  end</pre>
           <pre name="72e9" id="72e9" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">def users<br>    self.class.get("/2.2/users", @options)<br>  end<br>end</pre>
           <pre name="dc5b" id="dc5b" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">stack_exchange = StackExchange.new("stackoverflow", 1)<br>puts stack_exchange.questions<br>puts stack_exchange.users</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

           <p name="55e3" id="55e3" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/nylas/N1" data-href="https://github.com/nylas/N1" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">N1</em></strong></a>?—?an open-source mail client built on the modern web with <a href="https://github.com/atom/electron" data-href="https://github.com/atom/electron" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Electron</a>, <a href="https://facebook.github.io/react/" data-href="https://facebook.github.io/react/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">React</a>, and <a href="https://facebook.github.io/flux/" data-href="https://facebook.github.io/flux/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Flux</a>. It is designed to be extensible, so it’s easy to create new experiences and workflows around email. N1 is built on the Nylas Sync Engine, which is also <a href="https://github.com/nylas/sync-engine" data-href="https://github.com/nylas/sync-engine" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">open-source free software</a>.</p>

        <section name="68ed" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="8816" id="8816" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/airbnb/enzyme" data-href="https://github.com/airbnb/enzyme" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Enzyme</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em"> </em></strong>is a JavaScript Testing utility for React that makes it easier to assert, manipulate, and traverse your React Components’ output.</p>
           <p name="26e6" id="26e6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Enzyme’s API is meant to be intuitive and flexible by mimicking jQuery’s API for DOM manipulation and traversal.</p>
           <p name="8d5b" id="8d5b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing">Enzyme is unopinionated regarding which test runner or assertion library you use, and should be compatible with all major test runners and assertion libraries out there. The documentation and examples for enzyme use <a href="https://mochajs.org/" data-href="https://mochajs.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">mocha</a> and <a href="http://chaijs.com/" data-href="http://chaijs.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">chai</a>, but you should be able to extrapolate to your framework of choice.</p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

           <p name="d300" id="d300" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/facebook/flux" data-href="https://github.com/facebook/flux" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">flux</em></strong></a>?—?more of a pattern than a framework, and does not have any hard dependencies.
