           <h3 name="1a3c" id="1a3c" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># OCaml</h3>
           <p name="3c9e" id="3c9e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="07ce" id="07ce" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/the-lambda-church/merlin" data-href="https://github.com/the-lambda-church/merlin" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Merlin</em></strong></a> is an editor service that provides modern IDE features for OCaml.</p>
           <figure name="9e54" id="9e54" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">

         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="545a" id="545a" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/coq/coq" data-href="https://github.com/coq/coq" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Coq</em></strong></a> is a formal proof management system. It provides a formal language to write mathematical definitions, executable algorithms and theorems together with an environment for semi-interactive development of machine-checked proofs.</p>
           <figure name="1809" id="1809" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 200px; max-height: 200px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 100%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*aPH6qIRV-1xlUZat.png" data-width="200" data-height="200">

              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*aPH6qIRV-1xlUZat.png">

          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="20c2" id="20c2" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Haskell</h3>
           <p name="85b6" id="85b6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="073f" id="073f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/jgm/pandoc" data-href="https://github.com/jgm/pandoc" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Pandoc</em></strong></a> is a Haskell library for converting from one markup format to another, and a command-line tool that uses this library. It can read Markdown, CommonMark, PHP Markdown Extra, GitHub-Flavored Markdown, MultiMarkdown, and (subsets of) Textile, reStructuredText, HTML, LaTeX, MediaWiki markup, TWiki markup, Haddock markup, OPML, Emacs Org mode, DocBook, txt2tags, EPUB, ODT and Word docx; and it can write plain text, Markdown, CommonMark, PHP Markdown Extra,GitHub-Flavored Markdown, MultiMarkdown, reStructuredText, XHTML, HTML5, LaTeX (including <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">beamer</code> slide shows), ConTeXt, RTF, OPML, DocBook, OpenDocument, ODT, Word docx, GNU Texinfo, MediaWiki markup, DokuWiki markup, ZimWiki markup, Haddock markup, EPUB (v2 or v3), FictionBook2, Textile, groff man pages, Emacs Org mode, AsciiDoc, InDesign ICML, TEI Simple, and Slidy, Slideous, DZSlides, reveal.js or S5 HTML slide shows. It can also produce PDF output on systems where LaTeX, ConTeXt, or <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">wkhtmltopdf</code> is installed.</p>
           <figure name="86a5" id="86a5" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 379px; max-height: 373px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 98.4%;"></div>

           <p name="1fec" id="1fec" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/yi-editor/yi" data-href="https://github.com/yi-editor/yi" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">yi</em></strong></a>?—?a text editor written in Haskell and extensible in Haskell. The goal of Yi is to provide a flexible, powerful and correct editor core scriptable in Haskell.</p>
           <p name="9ef6" id="9ef6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Its features include</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="71af" id="71af" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">a purely functional editor core;</li>
            <li name="e4d8" id="e4d8" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">keybindings written as parsers of the input;</li>
            <li name="f011" id="f011" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Emacs, Vim and Cua (subset) emulations provided by default;</li>
            <li name="49dd" id="49dd" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li graf--trailing">Vty (terminal) and Gtk-based Pango UIs</li>
           </ul>
          </div>

           <p name="ee87" id="ee87" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/begriffs/postgrest" data-href="https://github.com/begriffs/postgrest" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">postgrest</em></strong></a><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em>PostgREST serves a fully RESTful API from any existing PostgreSQL database.            <h3 name="2370" id="2370" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Rust</h3>
           <p name="fcda" id="fcda" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="cc44" id="cc44" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/redox-os/redox" data-href="https://github.com/redox-os/redox" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">redox</em></strong></a><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?—?</em>an operating system written in Rust, a language with focus on safety and high performance. Redox, following the microkernel design, aims to be secure, usable, and free. Redox is inspired by previous kernels and operating systems, such as SeL4, Minix, Plan 9, and BSD.</p>
           <p name="0470" id="0470" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Screenshot:</p>

        <section name="17a4" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="1074" id="1074" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/weavejester/compojure" data-href="https://github.com/weavejester/compojure" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">compojure</em></strong></a>?—?a small routing library for <a href="https://github.com/ring-clojure/ring" data-href="https://github.com/ring-clojure/ring" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Ring</a> that allows web applications to be composed of small, independent parts.</p>
           <p name="165d" id="165d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Usage:</p>
           <p name="5729" id="5729" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">This small Compojure application demonstrates creating a Ring handler from two routes:</p>
           <pre name="0363" id="0363" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">(ns hello-world.core<br>  (:require [compojure.core :refer :all]<br>            [compojure.route :as route]))</pre>
           <pre name="ecac" id="ecac" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">(defroutes app<br>  (GET "/" [] "&lt;h1&gt;Hello World&lt;/h1&gt;")<br>  (route/not-found "&lt;h1&gt;Page not found&lt;/h1&gt;"))</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="6211" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="0e7f" id="0e7f" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/ztellman/aleph" data-href="https://github.com/ztellman/aleph" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Aleph</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em"> </em></strong>exposes data from the network as a <a href="https://github.com/ztellman/manifold" data-href="https://github.com/ztellman/manifold" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Manifold</a> stream, which can easily be transformed into a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">java.io.InputStream</code>, <a href="https://github.com/clojure/core.async" data-href="https://github.com/clojure/core.async" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">core.async</a> channel, Clojure sequence, or <a href="https://github.com/ztellman/byte-streams" data-href="https://github.com/ztellman/byte-streams" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">many other byte representations</a>. It exposes simple default wrappers for HTTP, TCP, and UDP, but allows access to full performance and flexibility of the underlying <a href="https://github.com/netty/netty" data-href="https://github.com/netty/netty" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Netty</a> library.</p>

           <p name="2de7" id="2de7" class="graf graf--p graf--leading graf--trailing"><a href="https://github.com/clojure/test.check" data-href="https://github.com/clojure/test.check" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">test.check</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?</em></strong>—?a Clojure property-based testing tool inspired by QuickCheck. The core idea of <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">test.check</em> is that instead of enumerating expected input and output for unit tests, you write properties about your function that should hold true for all inputs. This lets you write concise, powerful tests.</p>

          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="71db" id="71db" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/hoplon/hoplon" data-href="https://github.com/hoplon/hoplon" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">hoplon</em></strong></a>?—?a set of tools and libraries for making web applications.</p>
           <figure name="46a6" id="46a6" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 512px; max-height: 512px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 100%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*6UOR3E0vtVKAG2Eg." data-width="512" data-height="512">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*6UOR3E0vtVKAG2Eg.?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*6UOR3E0vtVKAG2Eg.">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*6UOR3E0vtVKAG2Eg.">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="cb0c" id="cb0c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Example:</p>
           <pre name="73e7" id="73e7" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">(page "index.html")<br><br>(defn my-list [&amp; items]<br>  (div<br>    :class "my-list"<br>    (apply ul (map #(li (div :class "my-list-item" %)) items))))<br><br>(def clicks (cell 0))<br><br>(html<br>  (head<br>    (title "example page"))<br>  (body<br>    (h1 "Hello, Hoplon")<br><br>    (my-list<br>      (span "first thing")<br>      (span "second thing"))<br><br>    (p (text "You've clicked ~{clicks} times, so far."))<br>    (button :click #(swap! clicks inc) "click me")))</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="512a" id="512a" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># C#</h3>
           <p name="3a36" id="3a36" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="06db" id="06db" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/tmenier/Flurl" data-href="https://github.com/tmenier/Flurl" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Flurl</em></strong></a>?—?a modern, fluent, asynchronous, testable, portable, buzzword-laden URL builder and HTTP client library.</p>
           <p name="efc1" id="efc1" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Example:</p>
           <pre name="882f" id="882f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">var result = await "https://api.mysite.com"<br>    .AppendPathSegment("person")<br>    .SetQueryParams(new { api_key = "xyz" })<br>    .WithOAuthBearerToken("my_oauth_token")<br>    .PostJsonAsync(new { first_name = firstName, last_name = lastName })<br>    .ReceiveJson&lt;T&gt;();<br><br>[Test]<br>public void Can_Create_Person() {<br>    // fake &amp; record all http calls in the test subject<br>    using (var httpTest = new HttpTest()) {<br>        // arrange<br>        httpTest.RespondWith(200, "OK");<br><br>        // act<br>        await sut.CreatePersonAsync("Frank", "Underwood");<br><br>        // assert<br>        httpTest.ShouldHaveCalled("http://api.mysite.com/*")<br>            .WithVerb(HttpMethod.Post)<br>            .WithContentType("application/json");<br>    }<br>}</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="4d40" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="7164" id="7164" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/NancyFx/Nancy" data-href="https://github.com/NancyFx/Nancy" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Nancy</em></strong></a>?—?a lightweight, low-ceremony, framework for building HTTP based services on&nbsp;.NET Framework/Core and <a href="http://mono-project.com/" data-href="http://mono-project.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Mono</a>. The goal of the framework is to stay out of the way as much as possible and provide a super-duper-happy-path to all interactions.</p>
           <p name="dd2c" id="dd2c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Example:</p>
           <pre name="e22f" id="e22f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p graf--trailing">public class Module : NancyModule<br>{<br>    public Module()<br>    {<br>        Get("/greet/{name}", x =&gt; {<br>            return string.Concat("Hello ", x.name);<br>        });<br>    }<br>}</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="7624" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="2c37" id="2c37" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/SuaveIO/suave" data-href="https://github.com/SuaveIO/suave" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">suave</em></strong></a>?—?a simple web development F# library providing a lightweight web server and a set of combinators to manipulate route flow and task composition. Suave is inspired in the simplicity of Happstack and born out of the necessity of embedding web server capabilities in my own applications. Still in its early stages Suave supports Websocket, HTTPS, multiple TCP/IP bindings, Basic Access Authentication, Keep-Alive.</p>
           <figure name="ee2c" id="ee2c" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">

           <h3 name="3409" id="3409" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Bash/Shell</h3>
           <p name="6237" id="6237" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="7aa8" id="7aa8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/yyuu/pyenv" data-href="https://github.com/yyuu/pyenv" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">pyenv</em></strong></a> lets you easily switch between multiple versions of Python. It’s simple, unobtrusive, and follows the UNIX tradition of single-purpose tools that do one thing well.</p>

           <p name="709c" id="709c" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/dokku/dokku" data-href="https://github.com/dokku/dokku" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Dokku</em></strong></a> is an docker powered mini-Heroku.               <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*2L6kj4dbuMGhKber.">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*2L6kj4dbuMGhKber.">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="b69a" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="7931" id="7931" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/sobolevn/git-secret" data-href="https://github.com/sobolevn/git-secret" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">git-secret</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?</em></strong><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">—?</em>a bash tool to store your private data inside a git repo. How’s that? Basically, it just encrypts, using <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">gpg</code>, the tracked files with the public keys of all the users that you trust. So everyone of them can decrypt these files using only their personal secret key. Why deal with all this private-public keys stuff? Well, to make it easier for everyone to manage access rights. There are no passwords that change. When someone is out - just delete his public key, re-encrypt the files, and he won’t be able to decrypt secrets anymore.</p>
           <figure name="1006" id="1006" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 165px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 23.5%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*ksb58FDyPxbZ5869.png" data-width="1400" data-height="329" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*ksb58FDyPxbZ5869.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*ksb58FDyPxbZ5869.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*ksb58FDyPxbZ5869.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*ksb58FDyPxbZ5869.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>

           <h3 name="6379" id="6379" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># R</h3>
           <p name="b9f0" id="b9f0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="046a" id="046a" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/rstudio/shiny" data-href="https://github.com/rstudio/shiny" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Shiny</em></strong></a> is a new package from RStudio that makes it incredibly easy to build interactive web applications with R.</p>

           <h3 name="2b59" id="2b59" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading"># Scala</h3>
           <p name="c7f3" id="c7f3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">—?—?—?—?—</p>
           <p name="5ca2" id="5ca2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://github.com/gitbucket/gitbucket" data-href="https://github.com/gitbucket/gitbucket" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">GitBucket</em></strong></a>?—?a Git platform powered by Scala with easy installation, high extensibility &amp; github API compatibility.</p>
           <figure name="d085" id="d085" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 316px; max-height: 329px;">

              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>

        <section name="e713" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="a5c1" id="a5c1" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/twitter/finatra" data-href="https://github.com/twitter/finatra" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Finatra</em></strong></a>?—?a lightweight framework for building fast, testable, scala applications on top of <a href="https://github.com/twitter/twitter-server" data-href="https://github.com/twitter/twitter-server" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">TwitterServer</a> and <a href="https://github.com/twitter/finagle" data-href="https://github.com/twitter/finagle" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Finagle</a>. Finatra provides an easy-to-use API for creating and <a href="http://twitter.github.io/finatra/user-guide/testing/" data-href="http://twitter.github.io/finatra/user-guide/testing/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">testing</a> <a href="http://twitter.github.io/finagle/guide/Servers.html" data-href="http://twitter.github.io/finagle/guide/Servers.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Finagle servers</a> and <a href="http://twitter.github.io/util/docs/#com.twitter.app.App" data-href="http://twitter.github.io/util/docs/#com.twitter.app.App" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">apps</a> as well as powerful JSON support, modern logging via <a href="http://www.slf4j.org/manual.html" data-href="http://www.slf4j.org/manual.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">SLF4J</a>, <a href="http://twitter.github.io/finagle/guide/Clients.html" data-href="http://twitter.github.io/finagle/guide/Clients.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Finagle client</a> utilities, and more.</p>
           <figure name="9cff" id="9cff" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p graf--trailing">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 407px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 58.099999999999994%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*1ettbQZXcoyn7Ay3.png" data-width="1194" data-height="694" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="0*1ettbQZXcoyn7Ay3.png">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*1ettbQZXcoyn7Ay3.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*1ettbQZXcoyn7Ay3.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*1ettbQZXcoyn7Ay3.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="245d" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="f426" id="f426" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/scalatra/scalatra" data-href="https://github.com/scalatra/scalatra" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Scalatra</em></strong></a> is a tiny, <a href="http://www.sinatrarb.com/" data-href="http://www.sinatrarb.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Sinatra</a>-like web framework for <a href="http://www.scala-lang.org/" data-href="http://www.scala-lang.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Scala</a>.</p>
           <figure name="68ca" id="68ca" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 231px; max-height: 174px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75.3%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="0*nuXpCbOPgCQ7_95n.png" data-width="231" data-height="174">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/0*nuXpCbOPgCQ7_95n.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*nuXpCbOPgCQ7_95n.png">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/0*nuXpCbOPgCQ7_95n.png">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="b62d" id="b62d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Example:</p>
           <pre name="7ff7" id="7ff7" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import org.scalatra._</pre>
           <pre name="b9db" id="b9db" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">class ScalatraExample extends ScalatraServlet {<br>  get("/") {<br>    &lt;h1&gt;Hello, world!&lt;/h1&gt;<br>  }<br>}</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="19dd" class="section section--body">
         <div class="section-divider">
          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <p name="3e67" id="3e67" class="graf graf--p graf--leading"><a href="https://github.com/twitter/algebird" data-href="https://github.com/twitter/algebird" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">algebird</em></strong></a><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">?</em></strong>—?an abstract algebra for Scala. This code is targeted at building aggregation systems (via <a href="https://github.com/twitter/scalding" data-href="https://github.com/twitter/scalding" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Scalding</a> or <a href="http://storm.apache.org/" data-href="http://storm.apache.org/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Apache Storm</a>). It was originally developed as part of Scalding’s Matrix API, where Matrices had values which are elements of Monoids, Groups, or Rings. Subsequently, it was clear that the code had broader application within Scalding and on other projects within Twitter.</p>
           <p name="a531" id="a531" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Example:</p>
           <pre name="2f14" id="2f14" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">Welcome to Scala version 2.10.5 (Java HotSpot(TM) 64-Bit Server VM, Java 1.7.0_40).<br>Type in expressions to have them evaluated.<br>Type :help for more information.</pre>
           <pre name="c6a0" id="c6a0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">scala&gt; import com.twitter.algebird._<br>import com.twitter.algebird._</pre>
           <pre name="702d" id="702d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">scala&gt; import com.twitter.algebird.Operators._<br>import com.twitter.algebird.Operators._</pre>
           <pre name="f75e" id="f75e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre graf--trailing">scala&gt; Map(1 -&gt; Max(2)) + Map(1 -&gt; Max(3)) + Map(2 -&gt; Max(4))<br>res0: scala.collection.immutable.Map[Int,com.twitter.algebird.Max[Int]] = Map(2 -&gt; Max(4), 1 -&gt; Max(3))</pre>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <section name="fd78" class="section section--body section--last">
